&lt;a class=&quot;read-more&quot; href=&quot;https:\/\/www.ispringsolutions.com\/blog\/10-best-screen-recording-software-for-windows-free-and-paid&quot;&gt;Read More&lt;\/a&gt;"}</script> <link rel="alternate" type="application/rss+xml" title="Explore the eLearning world with us &raquo; The 16 Best Screen Recorders for Windows PCs – Free and Paid Comments Feed" href="https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/10-best-screen-recording-software-for-windows-free-and-paid/feed" /> <script type="text/javascript">window._wpemojiSettings = {"baseUrl":"https:\/\/s.w.org\/images\/core\/emoji\/13.0.1\/72x72\/","ext":".png","svgUrl":"https:\/\/s.w.org\/images\/core\/emoji\/13.0.1\/svg\/","svgExt":".svg","source":{"wpemoji":"https:\/\/www.ispringsolutions.com\/blog\/wp-includes\/js\/wp-emoji.js?ver=5.7.8","twemoji":"https:\/\/www.ispringsolutions.com\/blog\/wp-includes\/js\/twemoji.js?ver=5.7.8"}};
			/**
 * @output wp-includes/js/wp-emoji-loader.js
 */

( function( window, document, settings ) {
	var src, ready, ii, tests;

	// Create a canvas element for testing native browser support of emoji.
	var canvas = document.createElement( 'canvas' );
	var context = canvas.getContext && canvas.getContext( '2d' );

	/**
	 * Checks if two sets of Emoji characters render the same visually.
	 *
	 * @since 4.9.0
	 *
	 * @private
	 *
	 * @param {number[]} set1 Set of Emoji character codes.
	 * @param {number[]} set2 Set of Emoji character codes.
	 *
	 * @return {boolean} True if the two sets render the same.
	 */
	function emojiSetsRenderIdentically( set1, set2 ) {
		var stringFromCharCode = String.fromCharCode;

		// Cleanup from previous test.
		context.clearRect( 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height );
		context.fillText( stringFromCharCode.apply( this, set1 ), 0, 0 );
		var rendered1 = canvas.toDataURL();

		// Cleanup from previous test.
		context.clearRect( 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height );
		context.fillText( stringFromCharCode.apply( this, set2 ), 0, 0 );
		var rendered2 = canvas.toDataURL();

		return rendered1 === rendered2;
	}

	/**
	 * Detects if the browser supports rendering emoji or flag emoji.
	 *
	 * Flag emoji are a single glyph made of two characters, so some browsers
	 * (notably, Firefox OS X) don't support them.
	 *
	 * @since 4.2.0
	 *
	 * @private
	 *
	 * @param {string} type Whether to test for support of "flag" or "emoji".
	 *
	 * @return {boolean} True if the browser can render emoji, false if it cannot.
	 */
	function browserSupportsEmoji( type ) {
		var isIdentical;

		if ( ! context || ! context.fillText ) {
			return false;
		}

		/*
		 * Chrome on OS X added native emoji rendering in M41. Unfortunately,
		 * it doesn't work when the font is bolder than 500 weight. So, we
		 * check for bold rendering support to avoid invisible emoji in Chrome.
		 */
		context.textBaseline = 'top';
		context.font = '600 32px Arial';

		switch ( type ) {
			case 'flag':
				/*
				 * Test for Transgender flag compatibility. This flag is shortlisted for the Emoji 13 spec,
				 * but has landed in Twemoji early, so we can add support for it, too.
				 *
				 * To test for support, we try to render it, and compare the rendering to how it would look if
				 * the browser doesn't render it correctly (white flag emoji + transgender symbol).
				 */
				isIdentical = emojiSetsRenderIdentically(
					[ 0x1F3F3, 0xFE0F, 0x200D, 0x26A7, 0xFE0F ],
					[ 0x1F3F3, 0xFE0F, 0x200B, 0x26A7, 0xFE0F ]
				);

				if ( isIdentical ) {
					return false;
				}

				/*
				 * Test for UN flag compatibility. This is the least supported of the letter locale flags,
				 * so gives us an easy test for full support.
				 *
				 * To test for support, we try to render it, and compare the rendering to how it would look if
				 * the browser doesn't render it correctly ([U] + [N]).
				 */
				isIdentical = emojiSetsRenderIdentically(
					[ 0xD83C, 0xDDFA, 0xD83C, 0xDDF3 ],
					[ 0xD83C, 0xDDFA, 0x200B, 0xD83C, 0xDDF3 ]
				);

				if ( isIdentical ) {
					return false;
				}

				/*
				 * Test for English flag compatibility. England is a country in the United Kingdom, it
				 * does not have a two letter locale code but rather an five letter sub-division code.
				 *
				 * To test for support, we try to render it, and compare the rendering to how it would look if
				 * the browser doesn't render it correctly (black flag emoji + [G] + [B] + [E] + [N] + [G]).
				 */
				isIdentical = emojiSetsRenderIdentically(
					[ 0xD83C, 0xDFF4, 0xDB40, 0xDC67, 0xDB40, 0xDC62, 0xDB40, 0xDC65, 0xDB40, 0xDC6E, 0xDB40, 0xDC67, 0xDB40, 0xDC7F ],
					[ 0xD83C, 0xDFF4, 0x200B, 0xDB40, 0xDC67, 0x200B, 0xDB40, 0xDC62, 0x200B, 0xDB40, 0xDC65, 0x200B, 0xDB40, 0xDC6E, 0x200B, 0xDB40, 0xDC67, 0x200B, 0xDB40, 0xDC7F ]
				);

				return ! isIdentical;
			case 'emoji':
				/*
				 * So easy, even a baby could do it!
				 *
				 *  To test for Emoji 13 support, try to render a new emoji: Man Feeding Baby.
				 *
				 * The Man Feeding Baby emoji is a ZWJ sequence combining 👨 Man, a Zero Width Joiner and 🍼 Baby Bottle.
				 *
				 * 0xD83D, 0xDC68 == Man emoji.
				 * 0x200D == Zero-Width Joiner (ZWJ) that links the two code points for the new emoji or
				 * 0x200B == Zero-Width Space (ZWS) that is rendered for clients not supporting the new emoji.
				 * 0xD83C, 0xDF7C == Baby Bottle.
				 *
				 * When updating this test for future Emoji releases, ensure that individual emoji that make up the
				 * sequence come from older emoji standards.
				 */
				isIdentical = emojiSetsRenderIdentically(
					[0xD83D, 0xDC68, 0x200D, 0xD83C, 0xDF7C],
					[0xD83D, 0xDC68, 0x200B, 0xD83C, 0xDF7C]
				);

				return ! isIdentical;
		}

		return false;
	}

	/**
	 * Adds a script to the head of the document.
	 *
	 * @ignore
	 *
	 * @since 4.2.0
	 *
	 * @param {Object} src The url where the script is located.
	 * @return {void}
	 */
	function addScript( src ) {
		var script = document.createElement( 'script' );

		script.src = src;
		script.defer = script.type = 'text/javascript';
		document.getElementsByTagName( 'head' )[0].appendChild( script );
	}

	tests = Array( 'flag', 'emoji' );

	settings.supports = {
		everything: true,
		everythingExceptFlag: true
	};

	/*
	 * Tests the browser support for flag emojis and other emojis, and adjusts the
	 * support settings accordingly.
	 */
	for( ii = 0; ii < tests.length; ii++ ) {
		settings.supports[ tests[ ii ] ] = browserSupportsEmoji( tests[ ii ] );

		settings.supports.everything = settings.supports.everything && settings.supports[ tests[ ii ] ];

		if ( 'flag' !== tests[ ii ] ) {
			settings.supports.everythingExceptFlag = settings.supports.everythingExceptFlag && settings.supports[ tests[ ii ] ];
		}
	}

	settings.supports.everythingExceptFlag = settings.supports.everythingExceptFlag && ! settings.supports.flag;

	// Sets DOMReady to false and assigns a ready function to settings.
	settings.DOMReady = false;
	settings.readyCallback = function() {
		settings.DOMReady = true;
	};

	// When the browser can not render everything we need to load a polyfill.
	if ( ! settings.supports.everything ) {
		ready = function() {
			settings.readyCallback();
		};

		/*
		 * Cross-browser version of adding a dom ready event.
		 */
		if ( document.addEventListener ) {
			document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', ready, false );
			window.addEventListener( 'load', ready, false );
		} else {
			window.attachEvent( 'onload', ready );
			document.attachEvent( 'onreadystatechange', function() {
				if ( 'complete' === document.readyState ) {
					settings.readyCallback();
				}
			} );
		}

		src = settings.source || {};

		if ( src.concatemoji ) {
			addScript( src.concatemoji );
		} else if ( src.wpemoji && src.twemoji ) {
			addScript( src.twemoji );
			addScript( src.wpemoji );
		}
	}

} )( window, document, window._wpemojiSettings );</script> <!--[if lte IE 9]><link rel='stylesheet' id='modules_related-ie9-css'  href='https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/wp-content/themes/ispring-blog-flat-bootstrap/css/modules/related-ie9.css?ver=5.7.8' media='all' /> <![endif]--><link rel="wlwmanifest" type="application/wlwmanifest+xml" href="https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/wp-includes/wlwmanifest.xml" /><meta name="generator" content="WordPress 5.7.8" /><link rel='shortlink' href='https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/?p=9089' /><link rel="icon" href="https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/cropped-android-icon-512x512-1-32x32.png" sizes="32x32" /><link rel="icon" href="https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/cropped-android-icon-512x512-1-192x192.png" sizes="192x192" /><link rel="apple-touch-icon" href="https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/cropped-android-icon-512x512-1-180x180.png" /><meta name="msapplication-TileImage" content="https://www.ispringsolutions.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2021/04/cropped-android-icon-512x512-1-270x270.png" />  <script async src="https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=G-ZREFGECPCF"></script> <script>window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

b-button_blue_float-block">Explore iSpring Suite</a></div></div></div><div id="content_container" class="container narrow_container b-post"><p>Screen recorder, screen recording software, screencasting software, and screen capture software are different names for the same tool that lets you to record a computer screen’s output. While screen capture tools differ in price and functionality, most share several features, such as:</p><ul><li aria-level="1">adjustable video frame</li><li aria-level="1">cut-and-paste editing options</li><li aria-level="1">unlimited recording time</li></ul><p>Which screen recording tool should you use to make an effective video tutorial, create an online course, market your business to online customers, or even record a new maneuver in your favorite game? We researched and compared the <strong>16 best screen recorders</strong> for Windows (both free and paid) and present them for you here. We hope this article will help you choose the screen recorder for capturing video on your computer that will be the best fit for your specific needs. </p><p>If you don’t have much time for reading and want to avoid the lengthy process of choosing software, just download iSpring Suite. It will let you create videos like a pro — even if you’ve never done it before.</p><div class="table_wrapper narrow"><table class="bordered_table"><caption>The best screen recorders for Windows 10: Free and Paid</caption><tbody><tr><td><strong>Best Free Screen Recorders</strong></td><td><strong>Best Paid Screen Recorders</strong></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#free-cam">Free Cam</a></td><td><a href="#ispring-suite">iSpring Suite</a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#dvdvideosofts-free-screen-video-recorder">Free Screen Video Recorder</a></td><td><a href="#camtasia">Camtasia </a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#sharex">ShareX</a></td><td><a href="#filmora-scrn">Filmora Scrn</a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#camstudio">CamStudio</a></td><td><a href="#movavi-screen-recorder">Movavi Screen Recorder </a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#ezvid">Ezvid</a></td><td><a href="#my-screen-recorder-pro">My Screen Recorder Pro</a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#tinytake">TinyTake</a></td><td><a href="#flashback">FlashBack</a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#obs-studio">OBS Studio</a></td><td><a href="#screencast-o-matic">Screencast-O-Matic</a></td></tr><tr><td><a href="#debut">Debut</a></td><td>&nbsp;</td></tr><tr><td><a href="#loom">Loom</a></td><td>&nbsp;</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h2>Free Screen Recorders that Save Money</h2><p>Whether you’ve paid for numerous software after using trial versions and received nowhere close to the bang for your buck that was anticipated, or you’re looking to save some money, there are plenty of free screen recorders that can get the job done with satisfying results without emptying your pocket. A word of caution though: some vendors may require you to buy a paid version after you download their “free” software so you can get full access to its functionality. </p><p>We compiled the eight best free screen recorders in 2022 that successfully compete with the best paid screen recording tools.</p><h2>1. <a id="free-cam"></a>Free Cam</h2><h3>Ideal screen capturing software for making WMV screen captures</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Windows</p><p><a href="https://www.freescreenrecording.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Free Cam</a> is a very simple free screen recorder with a built-in audio/video editor. The attractive and intuitive interface lets you to record both the entire screen and a portion of your screen — you can adjust the size of the area you need to capture. Even though this software is free, it doesn’t place any watermark and is ad free. Besides, it has no time limits — you can record videos that are as long as desired.</p><div class="image_wrapper" style="height: 380px;"><img loading="lazy" title="Free Cam" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2020/02/ispring-blog-image-1582106867.png" alt="Free Cam screen recorder" width="700" height="380" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li>No watermark, time limits, or ads</li><li>Records voice-overs and computer sounds</li><li>High-quality resolution</li><li>Users can save videos as WMV or upload them directly to YouTube</li><li>Easily deletes unwanted video fragments </li><li>Removes background noise</li><li>Wide selection of audio effects</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li>Saves recordings to WMV only</li><li>No webcam recording</li></ul><p>Watch this demo to see what you can do with Free Cam:</p><div class="iframe_preview_wrapper narrow js-demo-iframe"><div class="iframe_preview"><a class="js-zoom-iframe active" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TyjAnB4DksI" data-width="800" data-height="600"><img loading="lazy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645533664.jpg" alt="Getting started with Free Cam" width="" height="" /></a></div></div><p><a href="https://www.freescreenrecording.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Download Free Cam now →</a></p><h2>2. <a id="dvdvideosofts-free-screen-video-recorder"></a>DVDVideoSoft’s Free Screen Video Recorder</h2><h3>The best screen capture software for recording Skype video calls</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Windows</p><p><a href="http://www.dvdvideosoft.com/products/dvd/Free-Screen-Video-Recorder.htm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Free Screen Video Recorder </a>is a full-featured but lightweight free screen recorder from a developer known for its free conversion software. It can record Skype conversations with no limitations and is therefore useful for Skype meetings and online conference calls. Also, different Windows applications can be singled out and captured as discrete elements. Included is a basic user-friendly image editor that is surprisingly helpful for attaining a polished look.</p><div class="image_wrapper" style="height: 354px;"><img loading="lazy" title="Free Screen Video Recorder" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2020/02/ispring-blog-image-1582106974.png" alt="Free Screen Video Recorder" width="700" height="354" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li>Offers a convenient screenshot feature</li><li>Different modes for recording your screen and video</li><li>Suitable for recording Skype conversations</li><li>Step-by-step instructions provided on the site</li><li>Available in 10 languages</li><li>Output formats include MP4, BMP, TGA, JPEG, PNG, and GIF</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li>Microphone sound recording only</li><li>Excessive ads may interrupt your work</li><li>Lacks coherent interface and built-in media player</li><li>May install unwanted software during download</li><li>Does not notify users if disconnection occurs</li></ul><p>Here’s a video on how to capture your screen with Free Screen Video Recorder:</p><div class="iframe_preview_wrapper narrow js-demo-iframe"><div class="iframe_preview"><a class="js-zoom-iframe active" href="https://youtu.be/FTwoQzCP_1c" data-width="800" data-height="600"><img loading="lazy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645533906.jpg" alt="DVDVideoSoft Free Screen Recorder" width="" height="" /></a></div></div><h2><span style="color: #3e464a; font-family: Roboto, tahoma, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 32px; font-weight: 600; letter-spacing: -0.02em;" data-darkreader-inline-color="">3. <a id="sharex"></a>ShareX</span></h2><h3>The best screen recorder for PC for those who need to share screen captures online</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Windows</p><p><a href="https://getsharex.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">ShareX</a> is an open-source ad-free tool that boasts almost as many advanced features as some paid screen recorders. Free 7-day trial.</p><h2>14. <a id="my-screen-recorder-pro"></a>My Screen Recorder Pro</h2><h3>Good screencasting software for those who need to distribute videos to their website</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Windows</p><p><a href="https://www.deskshare.com/video-screen-capture.aspx" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">My Screen Recorder Pro</a> is a feature-packed screen capturing tool that enables you to record a specific area of the computer screen, including the entire desktop, menus, cursors, and video with sound. It also lets you record your webcam or mobile screen in high-definition quality simultaneously with the desktop screen. Besides industry-standard AVI, WMV, and MP4, the screen recorder can save video in WebM, perfect for distribution or uploading to your website or blog.</p><div class="image_wrapper" style="height: 511px;"><img loading="lazy" title="My Screen Recorder Pro" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2020/02/ispring-blog-image-1582109544.png" alt="My Screen Recorder Pro" width="700" height="511" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li>Can record webcam or mobile screen, along with desktop screen recording</li><li>Video output to AVI, WMV, MP4, and WebM formats</li><li>Allows scheduled recording</li><li>Auto-upload recordings to any FTP account</li><li>Can securely monitor the screen in hide mode</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li>Has limited editing options</li><li>No animations and transitions</li></ul><p>To learn more about My Screen Recorder options and settings, watch this video:</p><div class="iframe_preview_wrapper narrow js-demo-iframe"><div class="iframe_preview"><a class="js-zoom-iframe active" href="https://youtu.be/M0PqDHQ11Cc" data-width="800" data-height="600"><img loading="lazy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645535138.jpg" alt="My Screen Recorder Pro" width="" height="" /></a></div></div><p><strong>Price:</strong> $129.95. Free feature limited trial.</p><h2>15. <a id="flashback"></a>FlashBack</h2><h3>A simple screen recorder with basic editing features</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Windows</p><p><a href="https://www.flashbackrecorder.com/home" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">FlashBack</a> is a full-motion-based screen recorder with a simple, handy interface. You can record your computer screen, along with webcam and mic, and then improve the recording with a built-in video editor by adding captions, arrows, images, and highlights.</p><div class="image_wrapper" style="height: 438px;"><img loading="lazy" title="FlashBack" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2020/02/ispring-blog-image-1582109654.png" alt="FlashBack screen recorder" width="700" height="438" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li>Records multiple monitors</li><li>Incorporates webcam</li><li>Allows you to add distinctive and custom watermarks</li><li>Quick upload to Youtube, FlashBack Connect or export as MP4, GIF, WMV, QuickTime, AVI, and Flash</li><li>Can zoom in/out and add blurs</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li>Difficult to modify existing demos</li><li>Import files only in FBR format</li><li>Does not track the movement of windows in use</li></ul><p><strong>Price:</strong> $49 for 1 PC. Free 30-day trial.</p><h2><a id="screencast-o-matic"></a>16. Screencast-O-Matic</h2><h3>A reliable video capture tool with a built-in stock library and secure video hosting</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Windows, Mac and iOS, Android, and Chromebook</p><p><a href="https://screencast-o-matic.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Screencast-O-Matic</a> is considered one of the best screen recorders that can be installed on different devices, including PCs, laptops, tablets, and smartphones. It’s fast, fairly easy to use, and comes with a video editor that lets you to personalize screen recordings and make them more attractive and entertaining. Unlike its many competitors, Screencast-O-Matic comes with a built-in stock library full of videos, images, and music tracks, cloud hosting for storing and sharing videos, and even collaboration and team management tools. However, this advanced functionality is available only for premium plan users. It lets you to upload your videos to YouTube, Google Drive, Vimeo, and Dropbox. There’s also a mobile app for Android and iOS.</p><div class="image_wrapper"><img loading="lazy" title="Screencast-O-Matic" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645532956.jpg" alt="Screencast-O-Matic screen recorder" width="700" height="476" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li aria-level="1">Does webcam and audio narration recordings</li><li aria-level="1">Comprehensive video-editing options</li><li aria-level="1">Automated Speech-to-Text option</li><li aria-level="1">Built-in stock library</li><li aria-level="1">Secure and private online backup</li><li aria-level="1">Collaborative video management tools</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li aria-level="1">The free version embeds a watermark in videos</li><li aria-level="1">The free version limits screen recording time to 15 minutes</li></ul><p>Get more details about Screencast-O-Matic from this video:</p><div class="iframe_preview_wrapper narrow js-demo-iframe"><div class="iframe_preview"><a class="js-zoom-iframe active" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rZf-C05kZyQ" data-width="800" data-height="600"><img loading="lazy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645535192.jpg" alt="Screencast-O-Matic screen recorder" width="" height="" /></a></div></div><p><strong>Price:</strong> Pricing starts at $4.00/month. There’s also a free version with limited functionality.</p><h2>Comparison Chart of Paid Screen Recorders</h2><div class="table_wrapper narrow"><table class="bordered_table" style="width: 700px;"><caption>Paid screen recorder feature comparison</caption><tbody><tr><td style="width: 147px;">Product name</td><td style="width: 117px;">Webcam recording</td><td style="width: 104.938px;">Audio recording</td><td style="width: 96.0625px;">Video editing</td><td style="width: 233px;">Output</td></tr><tr><td style="width: 147px;">10. iSpring Suite</td><td style="width: 117px;">Yes</td><td style="width: 104.938px;">Yes</td><td style="width: 96.0625px;">Yes</td><td style="width: 233px;">MP4, HTML5</td></tr><tr><td style="width: 147px;">11. Here are a few solutions we consider worth mentioning. </p><h2>Zappy</h2><h3>The best screen recorder for Mac designed for remote teams</h3><p><strong>OS:</strong> Mac</p><p><a href="https://zapier.com/zappy" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Zappy</a> is software produced by Zapier, a company that provides workflows to automate the use of web applications together, specifically to improve communication and productivity within the company. It allows employees to create screencasts, screenshots, and GIFs easily, upload files to the cloud, and share each file with colleagues by embedding a link to G-Suite tools, Slack, and other services. The software doesn’t have a video editor, but lets you place colorful text, add arrows, or draw, so you can communicate with your peers visually.</p><div class="image_wrapper"><img loading="lazy" title="Zappy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645533429.jpg" alt="Zappy screen recorder" width="700" height="497" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li aria-level="1">Makes screencasts, screenshots, and GIFs quickly</li><li aria-level="1">Allows you to make annotations instantly</li><li aria-level="1">Enables you to add audios and a selfie view</li><li aria-level="1">Free cloud hosting with a paid Zapier account</li><li aria-level="1">You can highlight what’s important with an annotation or drawing</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li aria-level="1">No animations and effects</li><li aria-level="1">Only available on macOS</li><li aria-level="1">In the early access phase</li><li aria-level="1">Uploading captures to the cloud is a paid feature</li></ul><p>Watch this 20-second video on how this tool works:</p><div class="iframe_preview_wrapper narrow js-demo-iframe"><div class="iframe_preview"><a class="js-zoom-iframe active" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2RxpMEHxsxk" data-width="800" data-height="600"><img loading="lazy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645535216.jpg" alt="Zappy screen recorder" width="" height="" /></a></div></div><p><strong>Price:</strong> Free for paid Zapier users</p><h2>Apowersoft’s Free Online Screen Recorder</h2><h3>Free screen recording software that doesn’t require installation</h3><p>This tool is one of the few online video recorders. It lets you to record your screen and combine it with audio and webcam video. While recording, you can add shapes, notes, colors, and icons to your videos and then export them to various formats. When you’re done with the screencast, you can save the video to a local drive or upload it to RecCloud.</p><div class="image_wrapper"><img loading="lazy" title="Free Online Screen Recorder" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645533469.jpg" alt="Apowersoft’s Free Online Screen Recorder" width="700" height="354" /></div><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li aria-level="1">Doesn’t require installation on a computer</li><li aria-level="1">Simple interface</li><li aria-level="1">Webcam and audio recording</li><li aria-level="1">Unlimited recordings without watermarks</li><li aria-level="1">Support for live annotations </li><li aria-level="1">Multiple output formats</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li aria-level="1">Demands a stable internet connection</li><li aria-level="1">No animations or transitions</li></ul><p>To learn more about this tool and see how to use it, check out this comprehensive video guide:</p><div class="iframe_preview_wrapper narrow js-demo-iframe"><div class="iframe_preview"><a class="js-zoom-iframe active" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sIQqCzNdKmo" data-width="800" data-height="600"><img loading="lazy" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2022/02/ispring-blog-image-1645535290.jpg" alt="Apowersoft Free Screen Recorder" width="" height="" /></a></div></div><p><strong>Price:</strong> free</p><h2>How We Tested the Best Screen Recorders</h2><p>To prepare this detailed review, we installed each screen recorder on the computer and saw how well it performed. We expected to see the best screen recording software run smoothly on the PC and that the videos we created would play perfectly.</p><p>We also explored the functionality of each tool and compared their capabilities, assessed the user interface and whether the software is easy to use, and evaluated how closely each option meets the needs of its target audience.</p><h2>Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ) Section</h2><p>We’ve put together a list of common questions about screen capture software to take a deeper dive into the topic.</p><h3>What is screen recording?</h3><p>Screen recording, also known as screen capture, refers to recording anything that’s happening on your screen. It can be used for different purposes. For example, learning professionals can demonstrate to their employees how to use the software they need to perform their job. Software development companies can record videos on how to use their tool for their customers, and gamers can share their gameplay with the whole world.</p><h3>How to record your screen in Windows 10</h3><p>If you’re using the Windows 10 operating system, you already have an internal screen recorder called Xbox Game Bar. It has quite limited capabilities; more specifically, it doesn’t allow you to record the entire desktop or File Manager. However, you can use it with any desktop application or program downloaded from the Windows Store. Let’s see how to do this:</p><ol><li>Open the program you wish to record.</li></ol><p>2. Press the <strong>Windows</strong> key and <strong>G</strong> at the same time.</p><p>3. You’ll now see the Xbox Game Bar menu. Click on <strong>Start Recording</strong> at the upper left-hand corner of your screen. You can also capture your voice by clicking on the <strong>Microphone</strong> button.</p><div class="image_wrapper"><img loading="lazy" title="Xbox Game Bar menu" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2021/10/ispring-blog-image-1633963465.png" alt="Xbox Game Bar menu" width="700" height="258" /></div><p>4. Once you’ve finished recording, open the Xbox Game Bar menu and click on <strong>Stop Recording</strong>.</p><div class="image_wrapper"><img loading="lazy" title="Xbox Game Bar" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2021/10/ispring-blog-image-1633963556.png" alt="Xbox Game Bar" width="700" height="258" /></div><p>Congratulations! You’ve made your screen recording. You can find it in the <strong>Captures</strong> subfolder of the <strong>Videos</strong> folder.</p><div class="image_wrapper"><img loading="lazy" title="Videos folder" src="/blog/wp-content/uploads/editor/2021/10/ispring-blog-image-1633963579.png" alt="Videos folder" width="700" height="377" /></div><h2>Finding the Best Screen Recording Software</h2><p>Both free and paid tools from the best screen recording software can be effective methods of capturing the work-related or entertainment activities on your PC.</p><p>Whether you should spend money on one of the products outlined above depends on the nature of your tasks. Professionals working on an eLearning video project might benefit the most from <a href="/video-tutorial-maker" rel="noopener">iSpring Suite</a>. Experienced users with advanced technical skills might select the free ShareX screen recording tool. Those looking for a simple and reliable screen recorder for simpler tasks should be satisfied with Free Cam.</p><p>Did you like this article or have something to add to our review? Feel free to share your personal feedback and ask questions in the comment section. </p><h2>Further Reading</h2><p>Here are some more articles on this topic that you might find useful:</p><ul><li><a
